[12-Mar-2008 20:36:24] <loco> here is an example of one way you could do it steve.
[12-Mar-2008 20:36:27] <loco> exec .1.3.6.1.4.1.2021.56 value /usr/local/bin/ruby /usr/local/bin/grabstat.rb
[12-Mar-2008 20:36:29] <loco> in snmpd.conf
[12-Mar-2008 20:36:43] <loco> where grabstat.rb is a ruby script that returns an interger
[12-Mar-2008 20:37:18] <loco> then you can just graph .1.3.6.1.4.1.2021.56 as a custom snmp thingie
[12-Mar-2008 20:37:45] <loco> or exec .1.3.6.1.4.1.2021.57 vmusage /bin/bash /usr/local/bin/vmwatch.sh
